this international crisis.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9742a91e"><p class="cl-97427e58"><span class="cl-97427232">France</span><span class="cl-9742721e"> </span><span class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">Soviet support of Iraq was perceived by Kuwait, Iran, and other Western-aligned states in the Middle East as threatening.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91e4"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e40">Iran;Kuwait</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">experienced</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">a</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e40">fear</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">about</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e40">sentence</span><span class="cl-978e5e40"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e40">4</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-978e91ee"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">252.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">And Kuwait's growing rapprochement with Iran and Sa'udi Arabia disturbed Iraqi decision makers.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">No</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-978e91e5"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">252.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91e4"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">On 20 March 1973 Iraqi troops crossed the border into Kuwait, with a view to annexing part of the disputed territory along their 99-mile border.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91e4"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e40">Iraq</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">initiated</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e40">invasion/occupation</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">toward</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e40">Kuwait</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-978e91ee"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">252.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">Kuwait immediately sent troops, but they were defeated by the superior Iraqi forces, who then occupied the Kuwaiti outpost of Sametah where a number of huts were established.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p cabinet and parliament, a decision was taken to negotiate rather than fight.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">No</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span class="cl-978e5e2c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-978e91e5"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e2c">252.13</span></p></td><td refusal to do so, brought Riads efforts to a standstill.</span></p></td><td class="cl-978e91ef"><p class="cl-978e694e"><span class="cl-978e5e40">Iraq</span><span class="cl-978e5e2c"> </span><span
